BTANG BZUNG GI PHUG CES BYA BA YOD DO, ,YUL BE'U RA ZHES BYA BA
NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS

BZHUGS PA'I GNAS THUB CES BYA BA KLUS BTZUGS PA YOD DO, ,YUL KAM
PO TZA NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I GNAS
BYAMS PAS 'PHAGS PA ZHES BYA

BA YOD DO, ,RGYA'I GNAS NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS
BZHUGS PA'I GNAS MTHU BO THU'I PHUG CES BYA BA YOD DO, ,YUL KHA
SHA NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'

BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I GNAS PA LANG GI MGO BO ZHES BYA BA YOD DO,
,KHA CHE'I YUL NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I
GNAS SHIN TU STON PA ZHES BYA BA

YOD DO, ,YUL DGA' BA 'PHEL BA ZHES BYA BA NA SNGON BYANG CHUB
SEMS DPA' BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I GNAS GNAS BRTAN GYI PHUG CES BYA BA
YOD DO, ,YUL CHU 'DZIN ZHES BYA


@386A *, ,BA NA SNGON BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I
GNAS KHYOR BO STON PA ZHES BYA BA YOD DO, ,YUL SA 'DZIN GYI DKYIL
'KHOR NA

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BZHUGS BZHUGS PA'I GNAS BRGYAGS KYI PHUG CES
BYA BA YOD DO, ,SHIN TU RGYAS PA CHEN PO'I MDO, SANGS RGYAS PHAL
PO CHE ZHES BYA

BA LAS, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I GNAS KYI LE'U ZHES BYA BA STE, SUM
CU RTZA BRGYAD PA'O,, ,,
